They hope the government will resolve the situation quickly to avoid escalation.

Petitions from Beijing, Anhui, and Jiangsu 40

Nanjing, 23rd (Special Dispatch) - The Beijing Postal Workers' Union and the Anhui and Jiangsu Postal Employees' Union sent representatives, including Wang Shufan, to the municipal party headquarters and municipal government to petition, requesting that the central government quickly send personnel to Shanghai to persuade the Shanghai postal workers to resume work and order the Ministry of Communications to accept their proposals.

Chamber of Commerce Cables Hoping for Resumption of Work 41

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Nanjing Ministry of Communications, etc., yesterday, stating: "To the Nanjing Ministry of Communications, Shanghai Municipal Government, Municipal Party Headquarters, Shanghai Postal Employees' Union, and Postal Workers' Union: The postal service is the national transportation hub, and it is of great importance. With the Shanghai war just ended, order not yet restored, and the war zone preparing for reconstruction, the business community is settling accounts. Transportation services, in particular, cannot be suspended for even a day. Our Chamber previously telegraphed the government regarding the increase in postal rates, strongly advocating for a reduction. We have also telegraphed the Ministry of Communications to adopt the postal workers' suggestions, believing that the welfare of society requires that burdens be light and efficiency be high. However, the postal workers, because the government has failed to accommodate their demands, have implemented a strike, and the impact has caused nationwide anxiety. Delaying a decision will have serious consequences. We urge the government to take swift action and fully adopt the postal workers' good-faith suggestions. We also hope that the postal workers will prioritize the nation and society and resume work immediately. We especially hope that the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Municipal Party Headquarters will guide and assist in resolving the situation. We are sincerely praying for this. Respectfully, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Du and Huang Will Serve as Mediators 42

Du Yuesheng and Huang Jinrong, due to the postal workers' belief that the Ministry of Communications lacked sincerity in accepting the plan to consolidate the postal base, which led to the strike, are scheduled to host a reception for all sectors of society at the Taohuagong Restaurant on Mintini Road at 6 PM today.

Statement from the Savings and Remittance Bureau 43

Huadong News Agency reported that yesterday, the person in charge of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau made a statement to reporters, saying that the postal workers' demand to abolish the Savings and Remittance Bureau concerns the national administrative system. Whether or not to abolish it is a matter for the central government to resolve, and the Bureau has no position to take. However, there are still several misunderstandings in the outside world, and the Bureau must clarify them. (1) Postal employees believe that the separate establishment of the Savings and Remittance Bureau is the sole reason for the postal service's losses. In fact, the separation of the Savings and Remittance Bureau is completely unrelated to the postal service's losses. Apart from the Savings and Remittance Bureau being the hub for planning and promoting savings and remittance services, and the three branches in Beijing, Shanghai, and Hankou being the backbone for managing savings, all postal districts executing the orders of the Savings and Remittance Bureau to handle savings and remittance matters are still the postal service and its employees. The total annual expenditure of the Savings and Remittance General Bureau and its branches is only 639,661 yuan (accurate figure for the 19th year of the Republic). The progress of the savings and remittance business, combined with the total amount of savings and remittances, has increased significantly compared to before. Even if it is considered that the Savings and Remittance Bureau has no achievements and it is decided to abolish and merge it, the savings will only be over 600,000 yuan (in fact, it is less than this amount, because there are still some postal workers in the Savings and Remittance General Bureau and its branches who will still have to be paid by the post office after the merger). May we ask how much the postal service loses each year and whether saving this small amount can make up for it? Furthermore, the net profit of the Savings and Remittance Bureau is not transferred for other uses. According to regulations, after setting aside 30% for public reserve, it is still transferred to the postal service general bureau's account for use. In the 19th year of the Republic, because the postal service had more losses, the Bureau transferred all of its surplus of over 5,670,000 yuan to the postal service. Postal employees should all know this, but they still say that the separate establishment of the Savings and Remittance Bureau is the main reason for the postal service's losses, which is completely contrary to reason. (2) It is said that the Ministry of Communications established the Savings and Remittance Bureau to facilitate the withdrawal of funds. This point is even more unfounded. The Postal Service General Bureau and the Savings and Remittance General Bureau are both completely subordinate to the Ministry of Communications and must obey the Ministry of Communications' orders. If the Ministry of Communications wants to withdraw funds, there is no difference between the Postal Service General Bureau and the Savings and Remittance General Bureau. In fact, the Ministry of Communications has never withdrawn funds from the Bureau. There are records to verify this. Recently, the Bureau's Supervisory Committee has been established and has hired an accountant to audit the accounts. There will be a formal report in the future that can be used as proof.

Airmail and Telegraph Bureau Provide Temporary Services 44

Since the strike of the postal offices in this city, the China National Aviation Corporation, in order to maintain smooth communications, has devised ways to collect and send airmail as usual. It is reported that yesterday, those who went to the company to post were extremely crowded, and all the company's personnel were insufficient. Therefore, starting today, all airmail will be collected and sent by the wired telegraph offices and wireless telegraph offices in this city, as well as the Postal Savings and Remittance General Bureau.

Declaration from the Press Labor Union 45

The Shanghai Press Labor Union's Declaration on the Postal Workers' Strike states: "The resounding Shanghai postal workers' strike has finally erupted after brewing for some time. The long-term and short-term causes of this strike have been reported in detail from all sides. From these many detailed reports, we clearly understand that this postal workers' strike is entirely out of a desire to protect the postal service and to fight to save it. We express our deepest sympathy for this selfless and brave spirit of sacrifice. But unfortunately, as we carefully review the situation over the past three days, we cannot help but feel frightened. Why? Look at the disruption of news from various places due to the strike. Anyone who deeply understands the reasons for this strike can see this. However, imperialists, under the guise of 'maintaining the free flow of news', have begun preparing to seize postal rights. If this preparation expands along with the expansion of the postal strike, then we dare to predict that the entire Chinese postal rights will be handed over to the tiger's mouth, and there will be no way to save them. At this time, in the postal workers' subjective view, they are indeed striking to save the postal service, but objectively, they have achieved the opposite result. Therefore, although we express twelve points of sympathy for this postal workers' strike in principle, if it continues to be prolonged under the current circumstances, the result may be more harmful than beneficial. Fortunately, since the strike, the authorities have expressed their willingness to fully accept the demands put forward by the postal workers, but the plan to save the postal service still needs to be discussed later. Now that the postal workers' own demands can be resolved, there is no chance that postal rights will fall into the hands of the tiger. Therefore, this strike no longer needs to be prolonged or expanded. We hope that the discerning postal workers and compatriots from all walks of life across the country will pay attention to this. Then China will be fortunate, and the future of the postal service will be fortunate. We hereby declare. Shanghai Press Labor Union."

We sincerely hope that the postal workers can take care of the social traffic order and not expand this unfortunate incident, and that it can be resolved quickly so that it will not hinder the postal service because of the protection of the postal service, and it will not affect the traffic order of the people, especially after the postal workers' strike, the Public Works Department took the opportunity to establish a temporary postal service to replace it. Shirakawa Undergoes Emergency Abdominal Surgery 48

His Condition Improved Slightly After Surgery Yesterday

But His Life Remains Highly Perilous

Japanese Commander Shirakawa Yoshinori's condition deteriorated and, by yesterday dawn, he was unconscious and barely breathing, gradually entering a terminal state. At 8 AM, doctors performed another blood transfusion, and his condition temporarily improved. At that time, Dr. Goto examined Shirakawa's condition and had performed ten blood transfusions, but the vomiting of blood and bloody stools continued to persist. If his condition was allowed to progress naturally, he would not be able to survive the night. Therefore, it was decided to perform surgery in the hope of a slight chance of survival. Goto then anesthetized Shirakawa locally at 11:30 AM and personally performed the operation, opening Shirakawa's abdomen. A cancerous tumor, the size of a fist, was found in the duodenum. The tumor was cut off and removed. The surgery took about an hour. After the surgery, the vomiting of blood and bloody stools stopped suddenly, and his consciousness was relatively stable. However, he was still unable to eat anything. Doctors said that he had a glimmer of hope. If there are no more changes within the next day or two, he may be able to escape danger. However, his life is still highly perilous at the moment. At 11:30 PM last night, the chief military doctor of the Japanese Army Hospital examined Shirakawa and saw that his complexion had returned to normal. The military doctor then announced to the outside world that Shirakawa would be able to safely spend the night. Outside, there were rumors about Shirakawa's death, saying that he had died at 11 AM the day before and that the Japanese side was secretly not announcing it. In fact, Shirakawa is still hovering between life and death, and the claim that he is dead is not yet true. His will was verbally given to Chief of Staff Tashiro on the 19th, who recorded it and established it.

Dentsu News Agency, Shanghai, 24th, a slight pause. At 10 AM today, the Shanghai Expeditionary Force Medical Department announced Shirakawa's condition at 6 PM on the 23rd: temperature 37.6 degrees Celsius, pulse 108, respiration 20. The condition at 6 AM on the 24th: temperature 36.6 degrees Celsius, pulse 120, respiration 24. The condition at 5 PM: temperature 37.6 degrees Celsius, pulse 108, respiration 18. Black and reddish liquid stool was passed twice last night at 9 PM and 10 PM. Hemostatic injections were given, and 200 grams of blood were transfused. Although he entered a state of lethargy last night, he would sleep and wake up, which was very painful. From 6 AM to 7 AM this morning, he continued to pass black liquid stool three times. The degree of anemia has increased, and his physical strength is gradually decreasing. His pulse is gradually deteriorating, and the power of his heart is also gradually weakening. His life is already in a worrying state. Another blood transfusion was performed at 8 AM.

京滬路昨通車 49

Service Resumes on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Yesterday

Trains Departed from Shanghai Once in the Morning and Once in the Afternoon

Today’s Train Schedule Remains the Same as Yesterday

Yesterday (the 24th), due to the complete repair of the tracks and other infrastructure along the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, Director Chen Xinghan and Chief of the Transportation Department Zheng Baozhao urgently ordered the resumption of passenger train services. However, due to the limited number of trains, only two direct passenger services to Nanjing were initially operated. The first train departed at 11:00 AM, stopping at all stations along the route. A total of 237 third-class tickets and 8 second-class tickets were sold, generating a total revenue of $264.46. The second train departed at 3:45 PM, operating as a special express train, stopping only at Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Danyang, and Zhenjiang. A total of 283 second and third-class tickets were sold, generating a total revenue of $822.14. Director Chen Xinghan and Chief Zheng Baozhao personally oversaw all operations at the station throughout the day. Today, passenger train services will continue to operate in the same manner, with the first train departing at 11:33 AM. Additionally, due to the ongoing clearance work at each station and the lack of storage space, passengers are requested to collect their luggage immediately upon arrival to prevent loss. The Engineering Department is working day and night to clear and dismantle the original sites of the damaged stations. At 9:00 AM today, Director Chen Xinghan and Chief of the Transportation Department Zheng Baozhao will take a special train to inspect the tracks, bridges, telephone communications, and other infrastructure at each station between Kunshan. They are expected to return to Shanghai at approximately 4:00 PM. Director Chen Xinghan of the two railway bureaus is scheduled to host a visit for reporters from various newspapers and news agencies to Zhenru, Nanxiang, and other locations at 9:00 AM today. The gathering will take place at the United Press Office before 9:00 AM, with departure scheduled for 9:00 AM.

According to Huadong News Agency, after the resumption of service on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway yesterday, the train from Nanjing to Shanghai also arrived yesterday. The first train was the 7:00 AM early train, originally scheduled to arrive at the North Station at 4:44 PM. However, due to the recent completion of repairs on the tracks and bridges east of Kunshan, the train's speed was slightly reduced, and it arrived at the North Station at 5:20 PM, only 35 minutes behind schedule. The train from Nanjing to Shanghai was hauled by Pacific-type locomotive No. G57, pulling eight passenger cars. The train was extremely crowded, with approximately 800 passengers, and a large amount of luggage. Upon disembarking, passengers were delighted to see the national flag with the blue sky and white sun emblem displayed outside the station gate. Furthermore, the second train from Nanjing to Shanghai, the 8:00 PM service, also arrived on time at 9:05 PM last night. This train was even more crowded than the previous one. The gates between the North Station and the boundary road, which the foreign settlement had originally scheduled to close at 6:00 PM last night, were reopened by the railway authorities upon the train's arrival to facilitate the entry of passengers residing in the foreign settlement.

Joint Association of Various People's Organizations

Telegram Urging Universal Impeachment of Wang 50

The Joint Association of Various People's Organizations sent a telegram to the entire nation, stating (excerpt omitted):

"Regarding the Control Yuan's impeachment of Wang Jingwei for illegally approving the Shanghai-Woosung Armistice Agreement, based on the National Government's Organic Law, the Legislative Yuan has the power to deliberate and decide on declarations of war, peace treaties, and other major international matters. The Executive Yuan's approval of the Shanghai-Woosung Armistice Agreement without prior review and decision by the Legislative Yuan is considered fundamentally illegal. Wang Jingwei, as the President of the Executive Yuan, should be subject to appropriate punishment for this violation. This righteous stance is clear as day. However, it is reported that Wang's side is still employing deceptive rhetoric, attempting to justify his actions by claiming that the agreement falls under administrative procedures, that there was no declaration of war and therefore no peace treaty to negotiate, and that the case was approved by the Central Political Council, negating the need for review by the Legislative Yuan. This is extremely arbitrary. The agreement is clearly based on the outcome of a war between the two countries. We ask, what is Shanghai? What is the agreement? If there was no war, why a cessation? What is the difference between a declared war and an undeclared war? Is it possible to claim that there was no war when there were 32 days of bloody conflict, with the front lines extending for 200 to 300 li? Wang Jingwei's reversal of truth, his skillful sophistry, disregard the gravity of the matter and attempt to misrepresent the situation. He is truly a scourge to the Party and the nation. Wang Jingwei relies on the Central Political Council as his supreme backing, seemingly unaware that under the clear sky and bright sun, there is no such thing as an imperial court conference. Even if there are no capable individuals in the government and all departments are filled with sycophants, one cannot claim that there is no talent to be found. His contempt for the world is excessive. Wang Jingwei's guilt of violating the law and harming the country through the approval of this agreement is fully established. To be slightly critical is to call him a traitor, which is not excessive. The people of our entire nation are sworn to resist Japan, while Wang Jingwei is sworn to ingratiate himself with Japan, daring to act improperly and remaining unrepentant. Without a unified expression, it will be impossible to awaken him. (1) All organizations should jointly request the Legislative Yuan to declare that this agreement is entirely invalid. (2) All organizations should jointly request the Control Yuan to continue its impeachment, demanding that Wang Jingwei resign from his position, retract his approval, or face appropriate legal punishment. Furthermore, the government should announce its determination to resist for the long term and supervise its implementation. The prevailing trend of decline must be reversed, discipline strengthened, and the system reformed. The nation's future may yet be salvageable. Otherwise, if the Control Yuan stands alone and the Legislative Yuan remains silent, evil precedents will be set, leading to recklessness and impunity. The Party, the nation, and the country will perish, and great disaster will befall us. This association, mindful of these concerns, has voiced its strong opposition and issued repeated telegrams since learning of the impending agreement, expressing our extreme sorrow and indignation. We reiterate our call to action, urging you not to disregard this matter as a fait accompli." (remainder omitted) Respectfully, the Shanghai Joint Association of Various People's Organizations.

National Disaster Relief Association Telegrams Requesting the Suppression of Communists and Bandits 56

The National Disaster Relief Association sent a telegram to the Military Council of the National Government in Nanjing, the Governors of various provinces, the Pacification Commissioners, and military generals, stating: "Since the Japanese army invaded our territory eight months ago, the Northeast has almost fallen, and Shanghai has suffered repeated bloody battles. The entire nation is united in grief and indignation. As you command the troops and guard the frontiers, the nation looks to you with hope. It is your duty to defend the territory and strengthen the military, striving for survival. The people share this hope. Furthermore, the nation's quest for victory abroad must begin with internal stability. There can be no defeating strong enemies abroad when bandits and communists are rampant throughout the land. In recent years, communist bandits have wreaked havoc in our country, and efforts to suppress or appease them have failed. As a result, the people of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces have long suffered. Recently, half of Jiangxi Province has become a bandit zone, and they have even split into groups, attacking southern Fujian and northern Anhui. If this continues, they will surely grow stronger, and the nation will cease to exist, let alone resist foreign aggression. If you are truly motivated by love for the country and a sense of responsibility, you should seize this opportunity to vigorously suppress them, eradicating them completely. Furthermore, suppression must be done in cooperation with the people. We believe that the most urgent task is to quickly establish local militias in various places, based on the size of the villages and the number of people, organize them according to military systems, and implement training. They should be managed by impartial local gentry under the supervision of the local government, and the Party should not interfere, in order to unify authority. In peacetime, they can be used for self-defense and protection against bandits, and in times of need, they can cooperate with the official army and mobilize at any time. Their effectiveness will be far greater than distant reinforcements, which are often too late to be of use. As for the expenses, the local Party branches spend nearly a million dollars each year in each province, throwing money into a bottomless pit, which may even foster laziness and recklessness, harming the local people. These funds should be abolished and used to establish militias, so that the people can benefit and the villages can be defended. Recently, Guangxi Province has established militias throughout the province, with each team consisting of ninety people. Each county, depending on its size, trains several teams. Within a few months of their establishment, the bandit problem was eradicated. The organization of the Hunan militia is similar to that of Guangxi, and it has been recently reorganized with even better results. The fall of Changsha last year and the subsequent counterattack by the National Army, which involved fierce and bloody battles, are clear evidence of this. Now, Jiangsu has also entrusted gentry with the organization of a Defense Committee, which oversees everything and supervises the counties to actively implement the plan. Given time, it will surely be effective. At this critical juncture, when survival is at stake, we cannot afford to ignore this. The people must be able to live and work in peace before they can easily share a common hatred of the enemy, and the nation must be orderly before it can improve its politics. We urge you to be mindful of the danger of national extinction, fulfill your duty to protect the territory and the people, put aside all internal strife, suppress communists and bandits, and spare no effort. If the people's lives are hanging by a thread, they will be relieved, and if the nation's lifeline is not severed, it will gradually recover, reclaim lost territory, and resist aggression. This is the beginning. Please consider this carefully. Respectfully, the National Disaster Relief Association of the Republic of China."

British Residents Association Suggests Views of Various Foreign Chambers of Commerce 58

Opinions Still Not Consistent

According to the Continental News, since the British Residents Association proposed that various countries hold a meeting to jointly decide the status of the International Settlement and sent letters to various foreign chambers of commerce in the city to solicit their agreement, a reporter from the Continental News specifically inquired about the opinions of the various chambers of commerce yesterday. The British and American Chambers of Commerce did not wish to express any opinion. The French Chamber of Commerce is currently considering the matter in its board of directors. The Japanese Chamber of Commerce supports the resolution drafted by the British Residents Association and sent a reply letter yesterday. The Danish Chamber of Commerce has not yet made a decision. The Italian Chamber of Commerce is still considering the matter in its board of directors and expects to make a decision next week. News of Japanese Officers and Soldiers 59

Infantry and Aviation Unit 60

The Second Company of the 19th Infantry Regiment of the Japanese 9th Division, along with one artillery battalion and one aviation squadron, boarded the transport ship Harbin Maru at the Huangpu Wharf in Yangshupu at 11:30 AM yesterday and departed Shanghai for Japan.

Shigemitsu to Return to Japan 61

Ambassador Shigemitsu's injury has recently changed, and doctors have declared that he must be transferred to another location for treatment in order to fully recover. Ambassador Shigemitsu has decided to return to Japan by ship from Shanghai in early June for medical treatment.

Sending Personnel to Inspect Conscription 62

Every year, the Japanese Ministry of the Army sends personnel to Shanghai to inspect the physical condition of Japanese residents who are eligible for conscription. This year, Major Nishiwaki has been specially dispatched to Taiwan first, and then he will transfer by ship to Shanghai to inspect the physical condition of Japanese residents in Shanghai who are eligible for conscription. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday and is staying at the Tatsumi Ryokan.

Remains of the Bombay Maru 63

The Japanese transport ship Bombay Maru, which caught fire at the Huangpu Wharf, burned for two days and nights, and the military supplies and gasoline in the cabins were completely destroyed. Only the hull of the ship remains. The hull has also cracked, and the stern, where the fire was the most intense, has cracked and tilted and is about to capsize into the river. The Japanese military has dispatched two large barges with cranes to lift it up after it sinks.

Geneva Rumors Claim Investigation Team Favors Joint Administration of Eastern Provinces 64

Five-Member Commission Believes Only Solution to Break Deadlock

Administrative Committee to be Established with Zhang Xueliang as Leader

(Geneva) A surprising rumor emerged here today, claiming that the Lytton Commission intends to place Manchuria under the administration of the League of Nations. After considerable deliberation on all causes and effects regarding the Liaoning issue, the five members of the Commission believe that the only way to resolve the current deadlock is to place it under the jurisdiction of the League of Nations. This matter will be discussed in detail in the Commission's final report, which is to be submitted in September. As for the details of the plan, it is said that an Administrative Committee will be established with Zhang Xueliang as the leader, and representatives from Britain, France, China, Japan, or perhaps two or three other countries will serve as members. This committee will be responsible to the League of Nations. However, this rumor has not yet been verified in Geneva. Key officials in the League of Nations Secretariat have stated that they know nothing about this matter. (National News Agency dispatch from the 23rd)

Ma Zhanshan Prepares to Counterattack Tonghe 93

Telegram Recounts Retreat from Tonghe

(Beiping) According to sources in the city, Ma Zhanshan sent a telegram to Beiping yesterday, stating the following: "The Japanese army previously invaded Tonghe and was defeated by our troops led by Commander Jiao Jingbin and Commander Wu Linghan. After suffering losses, the Japanese army transferred a large number of reinforcements from Harbin by land and water. Jiao and Wu's troops engaged them in fierce fighting for more than ten hours, including hand-to-hand combat. Eventually, our troops were forced to retreat due to the enemy's heavy artillery fire. In this battle, the enemy suffered the loss of one lieutenant colonel, four captains, two lieutenants, and approximately seventy soldiers. Our army suffered the loss of Colonel Wu Linghan, commander of the 5th Infantry Regiment, Lieutenant Colonel Zhang Xinghua, deputy commander, two majors, six captains, and more than one hundred soldiers wounded or killed. The majority of our troops are now regrouping at Sanchan, more than ten li from the city, and are actively preparing for a counterattack." (Special dispatch from the 24th)

Central Government Held Regular Meeting Yesterday 100

Impeachment of Wang Approved for Handling by Central Supervisory Committee Resolution

(Nanjing) At 3:00 PM on the 24th, the Central Government held a regular meeting, attended by Wang Zhaoming, Chen Guofu, and over twenty other committee members. Committee Member Chen Guofu chaired the meeting and passed over ten routine items. The Central Supervisory Committee sent a letter regarding the Supervisory Yuan's impeachment of Executive Yuan President Wang Zhaoming. The letter stated that the Shanghai Ceasefire Agreement was not submitted to the Legislative Yuan for discussion and was signed hastily. After being presented at five regular meetings, it was resolved that the Shanghai Ceasefire Agreement was decided at the 29th meeting of the Central Political Council. Since this agreement is not a peace treaty, it should be handled according to the Foreign Ministry's proposal. It should be submitted to the Executive Yuan, and after completion, the Executive Yuan should report to the Legislative Yuan. Since this case has already been decided by the Central Political Council, the request to punish Executive Yuan President Wang Zhaoming should not be discussed. Please take note and handle accordingly. It was resolved to handle it accordingly. (24th Central News Agency)

Yu Youren and Wang Zhaoming, Heads of the Two Yuans, Submit Resignations to the Central Executive Committee 101

Central Government Urges Them to Stay with Sincerity

(Nanjing) Yu Youren, President of the Supervisory Yuan, and Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, both submitted resignations to the Central Executive Committee. On the afternoon of the 24th, the Central Executive Committee held a special discussion meeting. It was unanimously agreed that the Supervisory Yuan, in fulfilling its duty of impeachment, did not shy away from difficulties and exercised its authority, which fully demonstrated the spirit of independence of the country's five Yuans. The Executive Yuan's signing of the ceasefire agreement was also in order. As a result, it was unanimously decided to urge Yu Youren and Wang Jingwei to stay with sincerity. (24th Dispatch)

Zhong Ketuo Arrives in Bengbu to Investigate Embezzlement Case

(Bengbu) The National Government Flood Relief Committee recently allocated 200,000 yuan in relief funds to Northern Anhui, designating 11,000 yuan for first-class disaster-stricken counties, 8,000 yuan for second-class, and 5,000 yuan for third-class. Quan Shaowu, the Special Commissioner of the Northern Anhui Relief Office, changed the allocation, giving each county 2,000 yuan, inciting public outrage among the relief representatives of various counties. They believe he is attempting to embezzle relief funds and unanimously decided to drive him out to protect the relief efforts. The Northern Anhui Post-Flood Relief Association telegraphed Zhu Qinglan, requesting him to order Special Commissioner Quan to respect the order and distribute the original amount to each county to save the disaster victims. (24th Dispatch)

Foreign Important Telegrams

Saito Cabinet Formation Shows Progress 136

General Hayashi to Succeed Araki as Army Minister

Takahashi Retains Post, Economic Policy Unchanged

Suzuki Declines to Join Cabinet but Promises Assistance

Cabinet Members Largely Decided 137

China United News Agency, Tokyo, 24th: Saito's selection of cabinet members is progressing. Today, Suzuki, President of the Seiyukai, requested that Saito include Mizuno, Takahashi, Tokonami, and Hata in the cabinet. Saito only agreed to three. Mizuno, Takahashi, and Mochizuki are Saito's preferred candidates. The Minseito Party will nominate Yamamoto Tatsuo and Machida Chuji. Araki is determined to resign, and General Hayashi will succeed him as Army Minister. General Okada is determined to be the Navy Minister. Xiang Chengzhizhu, a figure in the business world, refuses to take office and recommends Nakajima Kumakichi to join the cabinet. Ucida, Yuasa, and Nagata, three members of the Upper House, and Hiranuma, Vice President of the Privy Council, will also join the cabinet. The distribution of cabinet members is roughly as follows:

Prime Minister: Saito Makoto (75 years old); Foreign Minister: Uchida Kosai (68 years old); Interior Minister: Mizuno Rentaro (65 years old); Finance Minister: Takahashi Korekiyo (79 years old); Army Minister: Hayashi Senjuro; Navy Minister: Admiral Okada Keisuke (65 years old); Justice Minister: Yuasa Kurahei (69 years old); Education Minister: Nagata Hidejiro (57 years old); Agriculture and Forestry Minister: Yamamoto Tatsuo (77 years old); Commerce and Industry Minister: Nakajima Kumakichi (60 years old); Communications Minister: Mochizuki Keisuke (67 years old); Railway Minister: Machida Chuji (67 years old); Colonial Affairs Minister: Kodama Hideo

Reuters, Tokyo, 24th: General Hayashi Senjuro, Commander-in-Chief of the Japanese Army in Korea, has been summoned to Tokyo today and is rumored to replace Araki as the new Army Minister.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 24th: Today's meeting of the three senior officials of the Army has decided to cooperate and support the Saito Cabinet. However, opinions on the successor of the Army Minister have not yet been unified and will be considered again tomorrow.

Seiyukai Promises Assistance 138

Reuters, Tokyo, 24th: Suzuki replied to the new Prime Minister Saito today, declining to take a seat in the new cabinet but promising to support it with the Seiyukai. Therefore, the new cabinet can ensure friendly cooperation between the two major parties in the House of Representatives.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 24th: Suzuki, President of the Seiyukai, visited Saito at 9:30 this morning to ask about the Seiyukai's assistance to the new cabinet and the new cabinet's policies on: (1) the gold embargo issue; (2) rural issues; (3) Manchuria issues; (4) the current situation; (5) the fundamental policy of organization. Saito replied that specific policies could not be stated at this time. However, (1) the gold embargo has already been implemented, and efforts must be made to prevent fluctuations in the economic world and there is no intention of lifting the embargo; (2) the rural area is plagued by social problems, and efforts should be made to revitalize it; (3) the established policy on Manchuria issues will be implemented; (4) the strategy to address the current situation is to stabilize the people's hearts; (5) the cabinet's organization policy has been detailed yesterday. Mr. Suzuki immediately understood and agreed to consult with the party's leadership before clearly answering whether to assist the new cabinet or not.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 24th: During the first meeting between Saito and President Suzuki this morning, the new cabinet's policy on fiscal and economic policies largely recognized the Seiyukai's policy and reached a consensus. As a result, President Suzuki decided to order party members to join the new cabinet and provide internal and external assistance.

Reasons for Retaining Minister of Finance 139

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 24th: Due to Saito's earnest request, Minister of Finance Takahashi decided to remain in office. Takahashi decided to take on the dramatic task despite his old age for the following reasons:

(1) Prime Minister Saito is an amateur in finance, so he must have a person with skills and personality as the Minister of Finance. (2) Minister of Finance Takahashi is a figure desired by the national financial world. Since the establishment of the Inukai Cabinet, he has been proceeding according to the planned financial policy. If he resigns this time, the financial world may be in turmoil. (3) If Minister Takahashi remains in office, the Seiyukai will definitely support the new cabinet.

Ogawa Does Not Recognize the Times 140

Only China, Italy, Germany, Russia, the Netherlands, and other 14 countries advocated for retaining the deletion. France, the United States, the United Kingdom, and others strongly advocated for deletion. Before the decision, the two sides argued fiercely. Representatives from China, Germany, Italy, and Russia all argued that dropping bombs would harm civilians and should not be allowed by humanity.

Sixteen-Year-Old Mystery of British Ship Bombing 149

Reuters, New York, 23rd – A person has been arrested here, and a diary has been found on him with the words "Killer of Kitchener" written on the cover. The diary found today contains a map showing the terrain of Orkney Island, with a cross drawn and the words "Kitchener killed here" written next to it. The location he marked is the site where the British ship Hampshire sank. The British ship Hampshire sank off the coast of Orkney Island, Scotland, in June 1916. At the time, Secretary of War Kitchener and his staff were on a secret mission to Russia on this ship. Unexpectedly, the ship had an accident at sea, and the cause remains unknown to this day, almost becoming a mystery. The person arrested today is said to have been a journalist and an international speculator. When South America was at war with Britain, he helped South America hate Britain. He was arrested here in 1919 for shipping several boxes on the merchant ship Denison, which was sunk en route, killing several people. Authorities suspected that the boxes contained explosives, so they arrested him. Authorities have not yet announced the person's name. Important News

Newspaper Discusses Japanese Reform Movement 151

Because the Party Government Relies on Zaibatsu

Impeding the Active Development of the Military

Therefore, First Overthrow the Party Government

The Nagasaki Daily News published an article by Xiang Hu Zhi on the 18th. The article is lengthy, and the following is an excerpt:

The assassination of Prime Minister Inukai, viewed from within, is not a surprising event. Why? Because the prime minister of a country, who controls the key to national affairs, is suddenly assassinated, it is naturally considered a major case. However, judging from past events in Japan, such as the attacks on former Prime Ministers Hara Takashi and Hamaguchi at Tokyo Station, although members of the Seiyukai and Minseito parties were very surprised, the general public showed no shock. Furthermore, incidents such as the attacks on Yasuda Zenjiro and Dan Takuma, although related to the zaibatsu and caused great anxiety, were also ignored by the general public. Moreover, in the past, the assassination of Ito Hirobumi in Harbin, and recently the bombing of General Shirakawa in Shanghai, did not move the public at all. However, Inukai's death was different. When the news spread throughout the country, panic arose immediately. For example, the stock exchange closed, and three prefectures outside Tokyo City temporarily declared martial law. All police officers nationwide were mobilized, which was unprecedented. The death of Prime Minister Inukai, who was approaching old age, by this ruthless bullet, was certainly imaginable at the time. However, the reason for the tragedy is not in this. Therefore, we should pay considerable attention to how the future situation in Japan will evolve. The surface cause of Inukai's death was a fatal blow from a huge shadowy figure. What is this huge shadowy figure? It is the current Japanese zaibatsu and capitalists. The entire structure of our country's government today is almost entirely formed by these zaibatsu. These zaibatsu, represented by two or three people, organize the government according to their own likes and dislikes, destroy the government according to their own interests, organize political parties based on their own relationships, and dissolve political parties based on their own well-being. For example, one side formulates laws, while the other side tramples on them. The decisions are made by their contradictory wills. For example, after the fall of the Minseito cabinet, the Seiyukai cabinet followed and re-prohibited gold exports in order to buy foreign exchange and accumulate tens of millions of yuan. They gathered the elite troops of the nation and sent them to war. As soon as the troops left our country's ports, their whereabouts were unknown, but the spies of the zaibatsu had already gone there first. This is the phenomenon that the Japanese military today is always under the control of the zaibatsu. Therefore, today's political parties and the military can be said to be two pillars supporting the zaibatsu. In the past, whenever a prime minister or president was suddenly attacked, the cabinet collapsed, or a political party split, although there was temporary unease, parliamentary politics and party politics did not waver in any way. When the leader of the zaibatsu was killed, although there was a temporary loss of control, there was no undue concern among the entire capitalist class. In the recent economic situation, in this era of extreme global poverty, if the zaibatsu do not invest, military spending will have to be reduced. The political parties with the zaibatsu as their background are naturally very arrogant. As a result, the military became resentful. Judging from the circumstances of certain major incidents in the past and the suppression of the Manchurian Incident beforehand, it can be proved that the person who killed the Prime Minister this time was a soldier, and was an organized group, openly wearing formal uniforms. Judging from their intentions, it was like wanting to pour boiling water on the backs of the zaibatsu and political parties. The reason why they took this drastic measure is that the zaibatsu and political parties today regard the country as a secondary issue, in addition to their own affairs. The general public is trapped in unemployment, worrying about the economic downturn day and night, while they spend all year round in gold and jade pavilions, wine pools and meat forests, without any pity. This aroused their great injustice, and they took this drastic action. From this point of view, the root cause of Inukai's death at the hands of the military is the intention to overthrow the current structure of the national society in order to reform it. The other day, Minister of the Army Araki said, "Investigate the root cause to prevent future troubles." What is the root cause he is talking about? That is, to smash the zaibatsu who ignite the people's lifeblood and covet fine wine and nectar with a heavy hammer, and overthrow them in one fell swoop, in order to wash away the filthy dust from the foundation of the party organization.

Zhejiang Postal Workers Unite with Shanghai Postal Workers 152

Implement Strike on the Morning of the 24th

Hangzhou News – Since the Shanghai postal workers' postal rescue movement occurred, and a strike was implemented on the 22nd, the close proximity of Shanghai and Hangzhou has had an impact. The postal workers of Zhejiang Province took unified action with Shanghai starting at 6:00 AM on the 24th. The situation is recorded as follows:

Brief History of the Union: The Hangzhou Postal Workers Union was established in 1927 and was organized by lower-level employees. It once went on strike and fought to drive out a British局長. Later, it was suspended for some reason. Urged by the Shanghai Postal Workers General Union, it was established on December 31st of last year. All postal workers in the province have joined, and the organization is quite strict. There are a total of 135 postal branch offices in Zhejiang Province, 6 branch offices in Hangzhou City, and a total of more than 1,000 employees.

Preparations: The Zhejiang Provincial Postal Workers Federation is located at the Guankou Branch Office. After receiving the news of the Shanghai strike, because the four items of the postal base consolidation plan were not accepted by the Ministry, the Federation prepared to respond and take unified action with Shanghai to show its determination to support postal rights. By the evening of the 23rd, a strike was declared.

Strike Declaration: The Zhejiang Postal Workers Federation's strike declaration stated: "Under the leadership of the National Postal Workers General Union and the General Labor Union, in order to save the postal crisis and express our unified determination, we announce a strike starting on the 24th and await orders. This struggle of ours is not for the benefit of colleagues, but for the entire postal industry, which has a great relationship with the people and the country. The postal industry can only be healthy and sound in the political environment of China by relying on the integrity of the organization and the independence of administration and economy. Unfortunately, since the recovery of postal rights, it has gradually been dominated by political forces and has shown a tendency to corruption. Two years ago, a few ambitious people wanted to seize the postal economic power and implemented a plan to place private individuals. Under the name of development, they forcibly separated the important parts of the postal service, savings and remittance business, and established parallel management agencies. This is the current Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau. Branch offices were established successively in Nanjing, Shanghai, Hankou and other places. In reality, the land-based savings and remittance business is still handled concurrently by postal departments in various places. However, the organization and system of the postal service have been broken since then. The use of personnel and administration by the Savings and Remittance Bureau is even more unbearable. The annual expenditure has increased by more than 3 million yuan. At the same time, airlines were opened, and the postal service subsidizes more than 1 million yuan each year. Such extravagance has led to the current postal losses and the implementation of this postage increase. However, the postage increase only makes the people suffer, and the postal service itself does not benefit at all. How long can the life of the postal service be extended by continuing to 'cut flesh to mend sores'? Therefore, Shanghai postal colleagues felt the darkness of the future and the importance of their responsibilities. On the 1st of this month, they gathered the opinions of colleagues across the country and submitted a 'Specific Plan for Consolidating the Postal Base' to the transportation authorities, requesting the following points: (1) Abolish the Savings and Remittance Bureau, and the savings and remittance business will still be managed by the postal department; (2) Stop subsidizing all expenses of the airline; (3) Temporarily maintain the original postage rates, and increase them after items 1 and 2 have been implemented and the postal budget is still insufficient; (4) Implement independent postal economy and special postal accounting, that is, use the postal economy to exclusively support the postal service; (5) Maintain the independent postal administration system; (6) Maintain the postal personnel system and guarantee the existing treatment of postal workers. Although there have been considerable revisions regarding the postage increase since the proposal of this plan, the authorities have completely lacked the sincerity to accept the above fundamental requirements. For a month, postal groups across the country have filed petitions one after another. The Shanghai General Labor Union and the General Chamber of Commerce have also simultaneously urged the transportation authorities to adopt them. However, the authorities have not been moved at all. We cannot but admit that they have other intentions and are willing to destroy the postal service. Today, we received an order from the National Postal Workers General Union to take strike action by colleagues in this city starting at 6:00 AM tomorrow (24th) in order to promote the authorities' awareness and await a resolution. We will not resume work until the goal is achieved. We are seeking permanent benefits for the people and cannot but hope that the people will endure temporary inconvenience. Dear people, forgive us and help us!"

Education News

Important News: The E Province Government Strives to Resolve the Education Turmoil 157

Summons Teachers and Staff for Talks, Returns Resignations

Hankou Correspondence – The education sector in E Province, due to the rejection of Shen Shiyuan, has caused a strike and work stoppage, and more than 10,000 young people have unfortunately abandoned their studies. Governor Xia Doudong, in order to resolve the dispute as soon as possible, specially summoned representatives of the education sector for talks on the 21st, and recommended provincial committee member Kong Geng and Secretary-General Yang Zaichun to persuade them. It is based on the fact that Kong is a senior figure in central E, and his virtue and reputation are well-respected and respected by the education sector, and Yang once served as acting Education Director, hoping to influence them emotionally. At 10:00 AM on the 21st, more than 30 education representatives, including Wang Yizhou, responded to the summons and arrived at the government office. Kong and Yang received them. Kong first asked two points, one was why Shen was rejected, and the other was why it was necessary to strike because of the rejection of Shen. He also conveyed Governor Xia's opinions, one to cancel the rejection of Shen, and the other to resume classes immediately. Education representative He Qingming expressed that the rejection of Shen was a matter of personality and career. Wang Yizhou said that he hoped the provincial government would approve the resignation and issue the back wages. Kong and Yang repeatedly persuaded them to take the students' studies as the priority and resume classes immediately, and returned the resignations on the spot. The representatives firmly refused to accept them. At the same time, they solemnly stated that resignation was not a strike. After talking for a long time, they dispersed without any result. At 12:00 noon, more than 30 teacher and staff representatives, including Luo Bingshu, went to the Education Bureau to demand back wages. The new Education Director Shen Shiyuan personally came out to meet them. Luo and others recounted their difficulties and said that Shen came with a plan and had his own appropriate methods. Colleagues had already resigned from various schools and museums and asked to issue back wages as soon as possible so that they could change their careers. Shen replied that the right to raise and issue arrears was in the provincial government, and the Education Bureau had no possibility of advocating it alone. He will, to the best of his ability, submit it to the provincial government meeting for long-term discussion. After Shen replied, the representatives continued to state their plight and asked to raise and issue them as soon as possible, but there was no result. The provincial government, because the persuasion was ineffective, convened a temporary meeting at 3:00 PM and decided on two measures: one was for the government to earnestly persuade the heads of various schools and museums and teachers and staff to perform their duties as usual, so as not to let students waste their studies; the other was to order the Education Bureau to handle it properly, and to instruct the heads of various schools and museums, teachers and staff to work with peace of mind and resume classes immediately to comfort the youth's desire to study. The instruction said, "For instruction matters, after investigating the reports published in various newspapers in Wuhan for days, the provincial schools are in a state of strike. According to the joint names of the heads of various schools and museums, teachers and staff of the schools and museums have all resigned from various schools and museums and submitted requests to relieve the heads of the schools and museums, etc., to the government. Yesterday, the Political Affairs Conference decided to publicly recommend the government committee member Kong and Secretary-General Yang to represent the government and summon the heads of the schools and museums, etc., for earnest persuasion, and the submitted resignations were returned on the spot and filed. According to the report of the government committee member Kong and Secretary-General Yang, after repeated explanations, the heads of the schools and museums still refused to withdraw their resignations, their words were tactful and their intentions were determined, and they were afraid that the schools would not be able to resume classes for a while. The government deeply regrets this. After investigating and appointing officials, the central government has its own discretion, and all teachers and staff should abide by it. Now, they are resigning en masse, wasting the time of the students and delaying the time, and they should also feel uneasy. It has been decided by the government's temporary meeting, in addition to instructing the Education Bureau to handle it as soon as possible, to earnestly persuade all the heads of the schools and museums and teachers and staff to be aware of it, to work with peace of mind and resume classes immediately to comfort the youth's desire to study. We have high hopes for this, this order." (May 21st)

Date of Selection 162

Records of Striking the Bell at the Old Temple (5) - The Unswept Courtyard and the Studious Man 163

When villagers talk about me, they immediately think of bell-ringing, so they call me "Bell." Over time, "Bell" became my only name. However, what I do at the old temple is more than just ringing the bell. It's probably because the bell-ringing is closely related to the villagers, so they remember it firmly. As for other things that don't concern them, they don't pay much attention. My daily work, besides ringing the bell, includes fetching water and growing vegetables. Also, I empty the chamber pot for the monk. I do the fetching water and growing vegetables as seriously as ringing the bell, so I won't talk much about them for now. It's only the matter of emptying the chamber pot for the monk that I'm embarrassed to talk about but can't bear not to mention. I've been doing this work since I was six years old, and it's been almost ten years now. At first, I only knew that the smell of the chamber pot was a bit unpleasant, and I thought it was something that children should do. When the monk needs to use the Analects, he is also a follower of Confucius. He often explains to me, "When there is something to be done, the disciples take on the labor." He says that these things include emptying the chamber pot.

Recently, I've begun to have doubts: "The monk also has hands, why can't he empty the chamber pot himself? Sick people and old people should be cared for. The monk is young and not sick, why does he need me to serve him?" Thinking about this, I immediately picked up a pen and wrote four lines:

"I have a pair of hands,

To ring the bell and grow vegetables.

To empty the chamber pot for others,

Is not what a true man does."

That night, I made a great resolution: from now on, I will only be a public servant for the masses, not a personal servant.

The next evening, after dinner, the monk picked up the chamber pot, felt it was heavy, and knew that it hadn't been emptied. He called me into the room, pointed at the chamber pot with his opium pipe, and said, "Have you forgotten to eat? Empty it!"

I said, "I can't empty it!"

He said, "Have your hands rotted off?"

I said, "Where are your hands? Empty your own chamber pot!"

He was so angry that he aimed the opium pipe at my head and knocked it. I caught it with my hand, and with a snap, it broke into two pieces! He immediately sent a fist towards my chest. I took a step back, caught his fist with my right hand, supported his elbow with my left hand, and pushed him with a smile, saying, "Use your strength to hit people to empty your own chamber pot!"

When I caught the monk's fist and supported the monk's elbow, I could have easily pushed him to the ground and made him eat mud with a simple press. Why didn't I do that? The monk really couldn't beat me. My fist doesn't hit those weaker than me. Besides, my purpose is only to no longer empty the chamber pot for him. He attacked me, and I had no choice but to resist. I only needed to let him know that I was unyielding to force, so why show off my strength? The monk still didn't understand and said angrily, "Get out! The food in this temple is not for you to eat. Get out with your tattered cloth and rotten cotton!" After saying that, the monk walked out of the temple in a huff. I don't know where he spent the night.

I am waiting to strike the last morning bell, bidding farewell to my village friends, and then going to the wide world to earn a living.

Shanghai Track and Field Competition: YMCA vs. Great China University 167

The Chinese YMCA has a significant influence among the six giants, mainly because the university athletes have been eager to try their skills since the Shanghai Incident. Now, they will serve the YMCA and participate in this grand sports meet. It is scheduled to hold a competition against the athletes of Great China University at Great China University on Jiaozhou Road this Saturday at 1:30 PM for practice. Most of the Great China University athletes are also YMCA athletes. This competition is only a nominal distinction, and in reality, they are all one family.

The Association is Preparing to Restore the Shanghai Chinese Tennis Federation 172

Mr. Hong Xianfang Donates a Silver Cup as a Prize

First Committee Meeting on the 30th

The Shanghai Chinese Tennis Federation was established in 1926. The first members included Lotte, Youyou, Yu Kuai, the YMCA, and the Chinese Five Ball Association. Through annual competitions, it had grown to as many as eleven teams by 1930, which shows the federation's contribution to promoting interest in tennis in Shanghai. The prize for the federation's competition was a large silver cup donated by Mr. Hong Xianfang. The cup had been won by the Chinese Association and expired in 1930. Last year, it was suspended indefinitely. Fortunately, the launch of the Xianfang Cup competition prevented Chinese competitions from being interrupted. However, the long history of the Chinese Tennis Federation was interrupted, which was regretted by all the ball clubs. Therefore, it was proposed that the Chinese National Sports Advancement Association should find a way to restore it. The association has written to Mr. Hong Xianfang to jointly discuss the restoration plan. Now, Mr. Hong has generously agreed to transfer the Xianfang Cup from last year as a national competition prize and entrust the association to prepare for and continue the competition in order to restore the only Chinese joint competition organization in Shanghai. His intention is excellent. The Association has now written to Fang Bofen, Ling Xitao, Chen Shao, Gu Qingyu, Ma Detai, and Zhang Zizhen to serve as committee members. The first meeting will be held at the Deng Tuomo Hotel at 12:30 PM on the 30th to plan the implementation.

Shanghai Education After January 28th (10) Still 173

15. Dispatched Students 174

A society that is frighteningly arrogant and pitifully naive, that highly disregards "love" and highly values "sex," and youths who were originally to be relied upon as the backbone of the future, the current general university students, jumped out of the environment of all evils to reform it. Who knew that the university students in Shanghai would suffer hardship before graduating? Those from wealthy families don't need others to take care of them; they have their own ways to find "safety." But the poor students in ragged clothes and with nothing to their names, who usually barely make ends meet, have difficulty surviving after suffering unexpected disasters. Therefore, those who were preparing to save society now need society to save them. Thus, the general poor scholars have the organization of the "Shanghai Schools' Disaster-Stricken Students Association," which has its office in the East China Apartment on Wangzhi Road in the French Concession. There are 606 university students participating. They elected representatives to carry out activities everywhere. The Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau sent personnel to conduct registration of disaster-stricken students, preparing to subsidize their return to their hometowns. From March 28th to April 2nd, a full week, only 36 people came forward to register with proof of their original school attendance. Five were middle school students, and the other 575 university students disappeared without a sound, not knowing where they went.

From the table on the right, we can see that the suffering of students who came to Shanghai from afar is several times greater than those from the local area and those near the local area. The reporter knows that the Patriotic Girls' Middle School in Chenyuan, Jiangwan Road, fled in a panic during the war, barely escaping with their lives. All their personal belongings were stored in the school, which was then set on fire by the enemy on the grass field. There were three female students from Sichuan who were in a dilemma and suffered unspeakable pain. Finally, their principal put together a few dollars to buy a boat to return to their hometowns. This is what I know personally. There must be many other students who have suffered terribly. Alas! Who caused this to happen? The 36 registered students, after a thorough investigation by the government and an additional oral examination, were given pocket money, free tickets, travel expenses, and letters of introduction, and were sent back to their hometowns one by one. In reality, 32 students returned, and 4 students have not yet received the money to make arrangements for their return. Presumably, they are planning other ways. The total cost of sending them back was 321 yuan. Apart from most of the government allocation, the Guangzhao Association subsidized 90 yuan, and the War Zone Refugee Relief Association subsidized 50 yuan.

16. Children's Day 176

In a period of great seriousness and imminent disaster, how can we calmly talk about Children's Memorial Day? However, how can we not talk about Children's Memorial Day? The importance of children from a national standpoint far outweighs their importance from a family standpoint by thousands of times. Moreover, in China, which is shaky and full of disasters, the Municipal Education Bureau formulated the "Implementation Outline for Commemorating Children's Day in Shanghai Primary Schools and Kindergartens During the National Crisis," "Teacher's Homework Reference Materials for Commemorating Children's Day in Shanghai Primary Schools and Kindergartens," and "Slogans for Children's Day" on March 1st, amidst the urgent rumors of enemy attacks on Nanshi, and distributed them to the schools for compliance. On April 4th, Children's Day, it sent personnel to the schools to inspect and guide them. Now, I record a copy of the implementation outline and 26 waiting slogans for reference.

Implementation Outline for Commemorating Children's Day in Shanghai Primary Schools and Kindergartens During the National Crisis

1. In addition to holding commemorative activities in accordance with the teachers' prescribed methods this year, special national crisis commemorative materials will be added to arouse national thinking. 2. Teacher's homework: A. Lectures, the contents of which are listed below: 1. The meaning of Children's Day and the promotion of children's happiness; 2. The situation of Children's Day in various countries; 3. A brief history of Children's Day in our country; 4. The national crisis and Children's Day; 5. Anecdotes of revolutionary martyrs and ancient great men in our country when they were young. B. Parents' meeting or family talk meeting (with special attention to children's lives and the issue of children's status) C. Mothers' and sisters' meeting (with special emphasis on motherhood) D. Check children's physical condition E. Health competition or sports meeting F. Exhibition of children's achievements in this school G. Giving Children's Day souvenirs (such as stationery, books, etc., limited to students of this school or kindergarten) 3. Children's activities: A. Exhibition of armed toys B. Patriotic short plays or games C. Disaster avoidance and defense competitions D. Tea party or party for children in each school or the whole school E. Comforting wounded soldiers G. Children's automatic saving of pocket money to save the country (training children to start taking responsibility for saving the country on Children's Day) H. Outing to study nature I. Writing and posting Children's Day slogans, such as: 1. We want brave children 2. We want strong children 3. We want honest children 4. Children must exercise to defend the country 5. Children must study hard to become useful talents 6. Children must speak morality to become good citizens 7. Children pay attention to science, 8. Children should develop a spirit of great selflessness 9. Children should abide by order 10. We want children who are willing to serve the society and the country 11. We want children who help others anytime and anywhere 12. We want clean children 13. We want hardworking children 14. We want children who do things seriously 15. Raise the status of children 16. Children are the masters of the future world 17. Promote scientific child rearing methods 18. Childhood is the golden age of life 19. Children belong to the society and the country 20. Children's Day is a happy day for children 21. To love the country, first love children 22. Only with new children can there be a new China 23. Revolutionary martyrs are the role models for children 24. Children should learn from the brave soldiers who save the country 25. Protecting children is the basic work of implementing nationalism 26. Good children's education is the only foundation for a strong country 5. Schools may choose to implement the above items according to their circumstances, and may also hold various activities that can arouse children's noble interests, such as electing model children. 6. Each school should prepare a detailed report on the implementation of Children's Day and send it to the bureau for review.

In addition, the Shanghai Child Welfare Association has contacted many celebrities to write commemorative articles for Children's Day. Readers may not forget that Shanghai's major newspapers carried celebrities' handwriting on April 4th. That day, the Child Welfare Association also held a variety show. The masters watching from the audience were mostly the little brothers and sisters in the refugee camps. This year is their unprecedented first Chinese Children's Day. It is a pity that the commemoration in Shanghai cannot be carried out as they wish, nor can it arouse the attention of the whole society.
