Suddenly hearing the sound of planes coming from the sky, this spring again faced the beginning of disaster. How can a famous town be a scarred place? Fortunately, the entire city was not burned to ashes.

Science

Manufacturing Blue-Black Ink 251

— Translated by Yi Yun

Blue-black ink, also known as iron gall ink. It is made by mixing iron salts, tannic acid, and blue pigments. When iron salts and tannic acid meet, they form ferrous tannate, which is colorless. However, when exposed to air, it quickly oxidizes to form black ferric tannate. This is why the ink is blue when it is written and turns blue-black after a while.

To make it, place four grams of tannic acid in a beaker (glass beaker is also acceptable), add 300 cubic centimeters of water and heat until the tannic acid is completely dissolved, and then let it sit to cool. Separately, dissolve five grams of green alum (i.e., ferrous sulfate) in 100 cubic centimeters of water. If the liquid appears yellow, add a few drops of dilute sulfuric acid to restore its original blue color. Then, dissolve three grams of blue pigment in 200 cubic centimeters of water and stir to dissolve it. Add three grams of gum arabic (approximately 10 cubic centimeters) and then add five cubic centimeters of glycerin and one or two drops of carbonic acid (carbonic acid is to prevent the ink from becoming moldy).

Add the ferrous sulfate solution to the cooled tannic acid solution. Then add this mixed solution to the pigment solution. Then dilute it with 500 cubic centimeters of water. After stirring evenly, filter it with filter paper or summer cloth, put it into a bottle, and plug it with a wooden stopper. Then you can take it and use it at any time. (translated directionpapor)

I and my classmates made it according to this quantity before, and the concentration was very appropriate. It is really more than not as good as the goods sold on the market. If it is too light, you can heat it to reduce the amount of water in it. If it is too thick, you can add water to dilute it. If you accidentally get ink on your body, washing it with water is not effective, but washing it with lemon juice will remove it.

Note: The method of making ink has been published in a previous article in this publication. This article is slightly different from the previous method, so it is disclosed again on the right. - Editor

Various Colors of Pigments 252

Pigments are not only used for painting, but also as a major raw material for paints. They can also be used for dyeing and making inks, and their uses are very extensive. A detailed description is provided below:

(1) Prussian Blue: One gram of yellow blood salt and six grams of ferric oxide.

(2) Scarlet: Equal amounts of potassium iodide and mercuric chloride.

(3) Barium White: Equal amounts of barium sulfide and zinc sulfate.

(4) Chrome Yellow: Ten grams of lead acetate and six grams of potassium chromate.

Dissolve each of the above substances separately in water, then mix them together and let stand for a while. Filter, wash the pigment powder two or three times with water, dry it, and grind it to form pigments of various colors.

(5) Chrome Orange: Add a little caustic soda solution to chrome yellow and heat together to form orange color.

(6) Green: Mix barium white, Prussian blue, and chrome yellow to create various shades of green, from grass green to deep green.

Add a few drops of linseed oil to the above pigments, mix well, then add a few drops of turpentine to form paints of various colors.

The filtrate obtained from the previous filtration contains potassium oxide, potassium acetate, and zinc sulfide. It can be stored in separate bottles for other uses. Due to limited space, it will be described in another article.

Sheng

A Father's Sorrow 253

— Wu

Mr. Yi has been very poor recently. His own salary has long been used up, and he even has to borrow money from friends for pocket change. But a few days ago, he received a letter from his wife, saying that she and a three-year-old baby were both sick. Especially the lively and lovely child, now has almost only a last thread of life remaining... At the end of the letter, she repeatedly urged him to send money back immediately.

Of course, the main thing is to send money back. With money, he could send them to the hospital. Naturally, a foreign hospital would be the most reliable. If they stayed in the hospital, that adorable child would surely be saved. Ah! That adorable child!...

But where is the money? Where is the money? What's more, it needs to be sent immediately!

He visited all his friends, he thought over and over again in bed, unable to sleep all night. Finally, he came up with a solution: his wife still had a piece of Indian silk long dress left in the box, and his own lined robe was no longer needed. Humph! These should at least be worth fifteen dollars, right? This is just enough to help with the immediate crisis. But the lined robe was very dirty. If it wasn't washed first, no one would want it. Finally, he decided to send it to the laundry.

So he felt a little more at ease. However, his wife's thin, crying face and the child's weak breathing constantly floated in his mind.

After enduring four very depressed days, he took back from the laundry this piece of clothing that could save his child's life. He felt even more comfortable in his heart. An hint of a smile, not seen in recent days, couldn't help but appear on his face. But he still had to check it. If there were holes in the clothes, it wouldn't fetch a good price. But, oh dear, sure enough, unfortunately, there was a big hole in a very obvious place at the lower fold. Who would want this?... There was no way to think, he could only send it to the tailor shop again.

"Hey! Please fix this for me quickly."

"Okay, sir: come back tomorrow night to pick it up."

"Can't you do it any faster?"

"Sir! That's really not possible."

He had another sleepless night. As soon as he fell asleep, he saw that his child had already died, and his wife was crying hoarsely beside him. So he also cried loudly, tearing his hair and beating his chest... Waking up, he was covered in cold sweat. "Ah! Luckily, it was just a dream. But this is an ominous omen! But it will definitely be able to send it the day after tomorrow morning."

Upon waking up early in the morning, he prepared himself to anxiously wait until evening, with a heavy heart.

At lunch, he received another piece of bad news, which was that the postal workers were on strike. How could this be? A telegraphic transfer was impossible. Fortunately, he discovered in the newspaper that airmail was not on strike, but whether money could be sent was still a question... No matter what, wait until he had the money in hand tonight before saying anything.

The lights were on, he was at the tailor shop.

"Sir! I'm really sorry, we're too busy, everyone is rushing to make summer clothes. Sir's is autumn clothing. It's no longer necessary to wear it now, please come back in a few days."

"But... Ah!"

Did he explain? No, he still didn't. How could he have the nerve to say it? So he walked out of the store as if he had suffered a serious injury.

"Ah! My child!... I see your face!"

When he went home, his face was covered...

Peeping into the Kaleidoscope

Barristers 254

— Qi Hua

Recently, it seems that there are already enough barristers in Shanghai. We can see the signboards of "XXX Barrister," "XX Joint Law Office" everywhere, displayed in a dazzling array. However, the "barrister manufacturing plant" is still producing them in batches. I'm afraid that in the near future, there will be a barrister every five steps on the street, and a law office every ten steps, making it extremely lively.

The first thing a barrister does on the day they open their practice is to post an advertisement. The first and most fundamental topic is "protecting human rights." But to be honest, their sole purpose is really a matter of career.

Now let's study why barristers are so prosperous.

The first reason is because divorces are very prevalent in Shanghai. But in this drama of divorce, a barrister must be used. Later, the number of divorce cases increased day by day, leaving barristers unable to cope, so the number of barristers increased.

There are many rich people in Shanghai. As soon as an old man closes his eyes, several sons will start arguing about dividing the inheritance. If the division is not equal, they will have to consult a barrister. This is another reason.

There are many people in Shanghai who like to show off. Once they have some money, they want to hire a barrister as their year-round legal advisor. Some people even hire several. So the more people who like to show off, the more barristers are needed. This is also a reason.

Also, it's relatively easy to become a barrister. There is evidence to prove this. The number of students in our school who study science is always less than the number of those who study law. And they all attend classes after 5:00 PM. During the day, they can find other jobs. Their professors sometimes don't come to teach because they are all barristers and have extensive social connections. If friends invite them to dinner, they can't go to school. But it's very convenient for the students because they can also go home earlier. This is also a reason.

The above four reasons were told to me by a classmate who is a small-time lawyer. His father is a barrister, and his family wants two generations to be lawyers. I don't think the reason he told me would be wrong. He also said: "We most welcome inheritance division business. If we do it once, we don't have to worry even if no one walks into the office for three months."

The Bread and Butter Problem

Collecting Paper Ingot Ashes 255

— Azalea

"Collecting paper ingot ashes! Collecting paper ingot ashes!" We can hear it everywhere, and we can see a special appearance, even more comical than Charlie Chaplin on the screen, even more calm than Blaise Pascal, with a crooked braid that's decades old on his head, plus a Qianlong-era felt hat, a face the color of paper ingot ashes, 14th-century clothes, and a pair of genuine domestically-made straw sandals on his feet, with a bamboo basket hanging from his right shoulder and a dry tobacco pot in his left hand. If you were to ask an archaeology PhD to estimate, it would still be worth studying.

I will now talk about their bread and butter problem. There are a total of eight or nine hundred people who sell paper ingot ashes in Shanghai. They are from Shanyin and Kuaiji, no one else is. They say that this is a specialty of Shanyin. Among these eight or nine hundred people, only one hundred have their own capital. The other eight hundred people collect ashes every day and sell them to the furnace owners. There are more than ten furnace factories in total. The one with the most capital is said to be Mr. Xu of the temple, followed by Mr. Sun at Xuenongdi. The best paper ingot ashes can be used to melt tin for profit. When buying and selling, if the seller is not careful, they will have the goods switched out. Their main occupation is farming. When the fields are busy, they return to their hometown. Once the fields are planted, they come back again. They can not only enjoy the prosperity of Shanghai, but also solve their bread and butter problem.

Automobile News Special Article

Replacing Old Cars is Sweet 260

Now is the Time to Buy a Car

When the 1932 new car models were launched in the last quarter of last year, manufacturers immediately ordered their new automotive products to advance forward. By the time the auto show opened in January this year, cars of all colors and styles came in droves. This further confirmed the above statement. After the auto show ended, the situation became even more apparent in the following months. All manufacturers unanimously made a decision to use their new automotive products as a vanguard to fiercely attack the situation in 1932.

The mechanical improvements of the 1932 new cars speak for themselves. Engineers are well aware of the advancements in the new car engines. However, most car drivers are not comparable to engineers. They express their appreciation for the new cars, but they only know what the manufacturers say, namely, that the new cars are cheaper than the previous ones.

Potential buyers of new cars are told that the new 1932 cars are invariably superior to their predecessors. Therefore, they all want to buy them like crazy and judge for themselves. As a result, some of them purchased them and were overjoyed. Customers all say that the new 1932 cars are of exquisite quality and fair price, a great improvement over previous products. What customers are saying now is what the manufacturers promoted at the beginning of this year. What people are talking about is not the cars they want to sell, but the new cars they want to buy.

In addition to the basic value of the new cars, there are various improvements, such as comfort of riding and safety and convenience of driving. Improvements in the chassis, engine, and body are often unknown to non-mechanical experts, but they can increase the serviceability and longevity of the car. Various improvements can also increase the pleasure of use. The current prices of these innovative cars are still being considered by the general public. First, the price is lower than that of cars in previous years. Second, the current low price cannot remain unchanged for long. According to the opinions of the heads of various manufacturers, the price of new cars has to increase.

Since the beginning of this year, the price of cars has been reduced and increased. There is a prevailing opinion in the market that the price reduction of cars has reached its lowest limit. Therefore, according to the heads of various manufacturers, the only change in car prices in the future will be an increase. In addition, the US federal government will soon impose taxes on cars, which will automatically increase the cost of goods for dealers.

Therefore, some say that the best time to buy a car is now. In addition, it goes without saying that buyers can spend all their money to buy a new car. Once the idea of buying a new car arises, the problem of disposing of the old car will inevitably follow. Many people believe that it is wise to keep their existing car for another year. This view is correct for some people, but not entirely. Car owners often have the experience that a car is uneconomical to use at a certain period in its life. As it gets older, the cost of maintenance will inevitably increase day by day. Frequent repairs and maintenance will cost more than a new car.

Therefore, owners of old cars cannot ignore this problem. They must make a comprehensive calculation to determine whether it is more economical to maintain a car with many ailments or to buy a healthy and strong new car. The issue of safety must also be considered. Many old cars are a clear danger to the people in the car and to drivers on the road. If one can think about the occurrence of danger, then one should not overthink the concept of economic savings.

Anyone who has not bought a car or who always buys cars of similar prices may not know the prices of various cars this year. Car buyers can spend all their money to buy a new car. If one wants to buy a car, but dislikes its high price, one may wish to choose a car with a slightly higher or lower price within the same category. Car buyers can buy a small Austin for 330 yuan, or a Duesenberg luxurious car for 13,710 yuan.

Regarding the two types of cars with the above-mentioned disparate prices, it is not easy to classify the various vehicles in between by value. Some cars may have very low prices in one category, but they are very expensive when viewed in another category. Therefore, it is impossible to establish a clear boundary between various cars. It is very clear. However, generally speaking, the thirty brands of cars manufactured in the United States can be divided into several types: low-priced, low-mid-priced, mid-priced, mid-high-priced, and high-priced.

Except for a few types of cars, the price of low-priced cars is generally around 700 yuan, such as the four-cylinder Austin, the six-cylinder Chevrolet produced by General Motors, the four-cylinder and eight-cylinder Ford, the four-cylinder Plymouth, and the six-cylinder Willys Overland. The price of the small Austin is generally from 330 to 550 US dollars. The price of the Chevrolet has recently been reduced, ranging from 445 to 625 yuan. The new four-cylinder Ford starts from 410 yuan to 600 yuan. The V8 model increases by 50 yuan for each model, ranging from 460 yuan to 650 yuan. The 1932 Chrysler Plymouth is priced from 495 yuan to 785 yuan for the convertible sedan. The Willys Overland "Six" new car is priced from 415 yuan to 665 yuan. Cars priced from 700 yuan to 1,000 yuan are mostly listed in the low-mid-priced category. Some are less than 700 yuan, and some are slightly more than 1,000 yuan, but most are between 700 and 1,000 yuan.

Benefits. If the existing short-distance light rail train is properly streamlined, the total horsepower required to travel at a speed of 75 to 80 miles per hour can be reduced by more than half.

It is expected that the results of these experiments will lead to revolutionary high-speed train designs. The application of streamlining to trains may not be as extensive as its application to airplanes, but considering the past achievements, it is not difficult to imagine its future development in this area.

Looking back to 1910, when humans began to explore the sky, streamlining was first tested in the air. The resistance encountered was entirely air resistance, and the original box-like airplane was deemed unsuitable and changed to a streamlined shape.

Dr. Ames, chairman of the National Advisory Committee for Aeronautics in the United States, once said that full streamlining can reduce the resistance of an airplane by two-thirds. Then, any three-engine large airplane on the US air routes, if properly modified, can reduce two engines and still maintain the same speed as it currently has.

Observing the recent performance of the British Royal Air Force, it can be seen that today's aircraft manufacturers attach great importance to streamlining. In the research to strive for more complete streamlining, many new airplane styles that reduce wind resistance have been obtained. After this, there is still ample room for streamlining to develop in aviation.

French Minister Weildon and his 1932 Citroen six-cylinder car pictured at the French Consulate in this port 261

Streamlining of Transportation Vehicles (Continued) Left 262

However, streamlining is not limited to automobiles. Streamlining is also necessary for trains. The results of experiments by French person M. Charles Maurpin determined that air resistance is at least one-third of the total resistance experienced by trains. Therefore, if French trains are properly modified according to the principles of streamlining, the amount of coal consumed each year can be reduced by one million tons.

Several trains in continental Europe have already been somewhat streamlined. One is the "Golden Arrow" of northern France. Its shape is as strange as its name. The carriages are tightly connected, with a shiny aluminum conical tail trailing behind. The German "Schubert Liner" train looks like a giant fish. It moves by means of a propeller installed at the rear. Recently, it set a new speed record of 143 miles per hour. Even in the United States, rounded locomotives with chimneys and headlights hidden inside can be seen.

The Westinghouse Research Experiment Institute in the United States is currently testing the effect of streamlining on special express trains and light rail trains. Research director Dr. Theodore Strong is convinced that streamlining express trains can reduce wind resistance by two-thirds and the total resistance experienced by the body by one-half. Tie also feels that streamlining is not very important for large, slow trains, but it is very important for light rail trains. Currently, the landing gear and protruding parts of airplanes can increase air resistance by 50% or more. If the engine is not fundamentally modified and the speed of the airplane is to be greatly increased, then those parts must be removed or built into the body.

Streamlining in navigation, like in land transportation and aviation, is also beginning to make rapid progress. The main reason why steamboats can reach speeds close to 100 miles per hour is the reform of the hull style. Old-fashioned V-shaped steamboats drained a lot of water, which caused great resistance. Since being changed to a flat seaplane style, its speed has increased threefold.

Partial streamlining has been successfully applied to several huge outer wheel steamships. New-style boats with aircraft propellers will soon be traveling in German rivers. This type of boat pays special attention to air resistance. The shape, which has been streamlined by engineers to prepare it for aerial use, has achieved effective streamlining when used for low-speed travel on water. However, when applying high speeds, the resistance situation is very different. A boat traveling at 100 miles per hour experiences the same resistance as an airplane traveling at 1,300 miles per hour.

Streamlining has almost become a matter of common concern in the engineering world today. Streamlining has a wide range of uses, and its application to ordinary cars seems to be the most revolutionary. If our cars are properly shaped, they can travel twice as far per gallon of gasoline. If this is indeed possible, why hasn't it been done before?

The reason seems to be that since aircraft became popular, the speed of transportation vehicles has greatly increased, making it necessary to consider air resistance. Also, most car manufacturers were afraid that the unusual style of streamlined bodies would not be popular at the time, so they did not dare to make changes.

Some say that streamlining cannot be widely applied today because the slender streamlined shape wastes the internal space of the car and makes parking more difficult. At the same time, a famous engineer predicts that streamlined cars will be popular throughout the United States in the next few years, and points to the achievements Germany has made as the basis for his prediction.

Overview of the Features of the 1932 New Car Yu 263

The 1932 new car has already been launched. With the old replacing the new, all car dealers are doing their best to promote it, filling the market with new cars to replace the old ones that have been used up. Car manufacturers are working even harder to promote it, competing to describe the various advantages and improvements of their new cars, removing the old and bringing forth the new, constantly striving for perfection. Compared with the previous 1931 model, there are many improvements and reforms. However, to describe the main points, it does not go beyond the following four items: (1) extra smooth and quiet operation, (2) reduced noise from the body and moving parts, (3) more refined body and chassis construction, and a more comfortable driving experience, (4) increased speed and more economical use, and a better appearance. Therefore, the 1932 new car, apart from the minor improvements in style and appearance, its mechanical structure has improved, namely, its excellent operation and power transmission.

The progress of automotive machinery is developing with new wonders every day, and the greatest recent progress is the free clutch. Its impact on car manufacturing is like that of the automatic engine and four-wheel braking system in the past. Almost all new cars have adopted this free clutch device. In addition, several cars will be equipped with automatic couplings, which have the function of a free clutch. As for the transmission of power, various cars have shown great progress in this structure. The gear shifting is easy and smooth everywhere, and the convenience is incomparable to the four-speed control device that was called the greatest progress a few years ago.

Not long ago, a car manufacturer created a small car that placed the engine on two rubber pillars, calling it "floating power." The manufacturer of this small car is said to be modifying large cars in its own way. However, if the construction method of this new invention is not adopted in the 1932 new car, it will soon be given deep consideration and used in cars. The above are all important points. Other important details cannot be described at this time. All the new cars this year have been referenced. Now, let me briefly list their names, such as vacuum electrical spark management, vacuum pump, used to drive the windshield wiper, automatic engine, fuel cooling device, and double valve construction, with four valves for each cylinder. This greatly increases the speed and power, while the size of the engine remains the same and does not increase.

In addition to the above, in terms of engine manufacturing, hard heat-resistant alloys are used in the cylinder walls and valve seats. Aluminum pistons are widely used. The number of lead-containing engines is increasing, so all-aluminum cars will soon be realized. The 1932 new car uses a lot of rubber in its manufacturing, because it can maintain stability and facilitate the operation of the body. The noise problem of cars has always been a problem that car manufacturers have been eager to solve. The 1932 car has made great progress in reducing noise. All kinds of noises from the engine, chassis, and body have been reduced to the greatest extent. The gear meshing is smooth and quiet. All parts of the power transmission are calibrated, so the impact noise is greatly reduced. The noise at the rear of the engine is almost completely eliminated, and the noise at the front is also reduced by special devices.

The construction of the body is also special, which can avoid all crushing noises. The tenon joints are all made by local forging, which is different from the use of screws in the past. Others use rubber as a filling material to avoid vibration and noise when the body is connected. In addition, car manufacturers have used a driving management feature to ensure the smooth and comfortable driving. This was invented by a manufacturer, and three other manufacturers followed suit. Passengers who have this manager installed

Page 22

Can exert the comfort they want. On various different roads, they can increase or decrease the oil pressure in the water shock absorber to achieve a smooth ride.

The physical strength of the chassis is as greatly improved as the body. Either its size is increased, or its style and construction are changed. Every place can make the driver feel comfortable and safe. When it comes to appearance, the 1932 new car has the most reforms. Its overall shape is low, flat and streamlined, so the radiator is also designed in a low shape to make it look forward and beautiful. The windshield is also slightly tilted forward, forming a beautiful curve that is very symmetrical up and down. The sun visor has been replaced by a curtain that can be adjusted at any time. This is very convenient for the driver, because it can block the sunlight coming from the front at any time, and can also block the light coming from the side, making the forward view clearer. Moreover, removing the sun visor not only improves the appearance, but also makes the action faster, because it can reduce the pressure resistance of the wind. As for the symmetry and beauty of the front and rear shapes of the new car, there is no need to repeat them.

The internal form and beauty of the new car are all excellent, but one thing can be stated is that the driving buttons used on the new car are all installed directly in front of the driver. In this way, the driver can have the wonderful feeling of getting started quickly and with ease when looking forward. Moreover, the space on the right is freed up. This is a safety feature of the 1932 new car.

News Ford Motor's Recent Reforms Ze 264

The 1932 Ford car has only slight changes in its appearance in the water tank. Also, the body is lowered like a scholar because the front and rear axles are slightly bent downward. No other innovations have been seen.

As for the content of the Ford car, there are many reforms. The most important of these is the location of the gasoline tank, which has been moved from the front of the car to the rear. The reason why the gasoline tank is placed in the front of the car is that it is close to the engine, which poses a fire hazard. Except for very small cars, which cannot be moved, almost no cars have the gasoline tank placed in the front. Now that Ford cars have moved the gasoline tank to the rear of the car, the contents of Ford cars are becoming more and more similar to ordinary cars. As for the position of the gasoline tank being moved to the rear, a gasoline pump is added to draw gasoline into the carburetor.

The steering wheel of the new car is made of black copper bone elm skin. In the center of the wheel, there is a control for the front headlights. A lock is also added to the steering gear to make the car parked on the road safer.

The window wiping machine on the front window of the new car is also very novel. The machine uses the engine's intake function to move. The whole machine is hidden inside the roof, and even the steam pipe is hidden and cannot be seen. Only the switch and the wiper blade are exposed.

The lubrication system of the engine has been improved, that is, an oil pump is added to the original splashing method to supply oil, so that the circulation of the engine oil is more active.

The diameter of the wheels is slightly shortened, but the size of the tires is slightly increased, with measurements of 5.25×18 inches.

The length of the body has increased by two and a half inches. Therefore, the doors of the two-door sedan are very wide. Passengers who want to enter the rear seats in the car do not need to press down the back of the front seat, so entering and exiting is very convenient.

The contents of the transmission have also been slightly reformed. The gears in the second gear are constantly meshing, and the speed change is very simple. It is also stable and noise-free when used. The contents of the Ford engine are completely unchanged except for the addition of one gasoline and one oil pump each. The battery in the electrical group has a capacity of eighty amperes.

There are two types of Ford cars manufactured in the UK. One is the small Ford car with eight horsepower, and the other is the large Ford car. The latter is divided into two types: high power and low power. Except for the different horsepower of the engines, all parts of the chassis are completely the same. The selling price in the UK is £180 for the two-door sedan and £225 for the four-door sedan. If you buy a small horsepower car, you have to add another £5.

The above-mentioned high-power engine has an actual horsepower of 24 horsepower, and the low-power engine has 14 horsepower. The former generates 48 horsepower at a speed of 2,400 revolutions per minute, and the latter can get 41 horsepower at 3,000 revolutions per minute.

As for the low-horsepower engine, it saves more gasoline. If the current gasoline tank can hold 11 gallons of gasoline, it can travel 270 miles. However, the high-horsepower car can only travel 240 miles.

Features of Commer Trucks Explained 265

Commer Commercial Motor Car Company. One of the earliest established among the major British truck manufacturers. Its products have been popular all over the world for more than twenty-five years. Commer trucks' four-cylinder and six-cylinder engines are strong and beautiful, with no worry of vibration. They are used for heavy loads and long distances, and are extremely economical and cost-effective. They are not only agile and stable. As for the entire chassis, it is especially praised by engineers and transportation companies. The silent three-speed gearbox is a feature of commercial vehicles that originated with Commer, and has been proven by the "fG.Q" and "Jnvader" models. This is especially effective for difficult jobs. Only with this equipment can a proper speed be maintained, and less force is applied to the engine. Another important feature is that Commer trucks use a special superior worm gear as standard equipment, which is light, has no vibration, and allows the driver to control the vehicle freely and easily in crowded areas. The design of the new Commer truck

and construction are perfectly suited to modern automotive transport and all the needs of mechanical power ratio. There are two styles on display: the famous "Raider" and "Gentaur". The Raider has the most complete advantages of any one-and-a-half-ton truck in the same price range. The wheelbase is ten feet six inches. If equipped with a railing body, it is especially suitable for loading long and heavy goods. The engine is a side-valve type, with six cylinders and a Royal Automobile Club rated horsepower of 22.6. Public Concession Recent Automobile Statistics Praised 267

Ford Ranks First with the Most

The automobile registration statistics of the French Concession in Shanghai have been recorded in this publication. Here are the recent statistics of automobile registration in the Public Concession. From January 1, 1932 to March 31, the number of automobile registrations in the first quarter of this year was 6,038 passenger cars, 1,933 trucks, and 782 motorcycles. There were a total of 173 brands of passenger cars, but the automobiles used by the foreign troops stationed in Shanghai are not included, and the number is also several hundred. Among the cars, the largest number is still Buick and Ford. Ford is the champion, with a number of 642. Buick is 7 less than Ford, with a total of 635, ranking second.

In addition to Ford and Buick, the third is Chevrolet, with a total of 385. The fourth is Austin, with 372. The others with more than 300 are Studebaker, ranking fifth, with 339. Felix the Cat ranks sixth, with 334. Morris Cowley ranks seventh, with 317.

There are four types with more than 200. Dodge ranks eighth with 260. Nash ranks ninth with 260. Essex ranks tenth with 206. Willys-Overland Whippet ranks eleventh with 201. Those exceeding 100 include Morris Oxford with 182, Citroen with 168, Chrysler with 126, Hupmobile with 119, and Renault with 102. Judging from the above numbers, it is evident that Austin, Studebaker, and Standard are progressing very rapidly. Plymouth also shows signs of improvement. This kind of increase is quite similar to the situation in the United States. This is probably due to the progress of "floating power."

Advantages of Dodge Four-Cylinder Cars 268

Floating Power and Free Wheeling

The revival of Dodge four-cylinder cars is truly an important page in automotive history. Considering that automobile manufacturers are currently competing fiercely to be the leader, and want to use the increase in the number of engine cylinders to solve the problem of car vibration, then the revival of this type of four-cylinder car is especially valuable and worthy of praise. Four-cylinder cars have always been known for their simplicity and economy. Now, in addition to restoring its original characteristics, the Dodge four-cylinder car also has natural floating power. Because of this advantage, not only are all the shaking and vibrations of the frame and body completely eliminated, but also its full mechanical power, magnificent effect, comfortable appearance, and easy and free operation are all outstanding and unmatched.

In addition to natural floating power, free wheeling is another important feature of the new Dodge four-cylinder car. The reason why the new Dodge four-cylinder car is so easy to operate and has the advantage of "effortless management" is that it has a special superior power transmission device, silent gears, silent second gear, and free wheeling. The sedan-shaped double-drop frame, matched with a steel-welded unibody, complement each other and are even more beautiful. The center of gravity of the car is thus lowered, while the road clearance and interior position are not damaged at all. Furthermore, the use of a new driving wheel and a steering wheel shock absorber placed on the front spring to the left or right of the driver, so that road bumps will not be transmitted to the steering wheel, making it more comfortable to be in the car. As for high-speed driving, no matter how sharp the turn, it is still smooth and comfortable, with no danger of tilting or hard wheel turning. The reason why the new Dodge four-cylinder car is so easy to drive and so comfortable to ride is due to the above advantages.
